Tom likes to write short stories. Each night, he sits by the bright light of his desk lamp and thinks about new ideas. He might create tales about knights and their brave fights, or ships sailing through stormy seas. Sometimes he writes about space and planets far away. His friends say he has a great imagination.

Music helps people relax after a busy day. Different types of music can change how we feel. Some prefer classical pieces with piano and violin. Others enjoy modern songs with strong beats and catchy tunes. Many students listen to gentle music while they study. Research shows that certain music can improve our focus and memory.

é‡ç‚¹ï¼šæ³¨æ„åè¯ã€åŠ¨è¯å’Œå½¢å®¹è¯çš„é‡è¯»ï¼Œå¥å­çš„èŠ‚å¥æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œä»¥åŠå¤šéŸ³èŠ‚è¯çš„é‡éŸ³ã€‚

The ancient castle stood high on the mountain, its stone walls weathered by centuries of wind and rain. Knights once guarded its chambers and halls, while noble ladies walked through beautiful gardens nearby. Children would listen eagerly to tales of dragons and adventures, their eyes wide with wonder at the thought of treasure hidden somewhere beneath the castle grounds.

Today, tourists from around the world climb the steep path to explore this historical site. They photograph the magnificent architecture and imagine what life was like in medieval times. Guides explain how people cooked their meals, designed their furniture, and entertained themselves without modern technology. Despite its age, the castle continues to inspire awe in everyone who visits.

ç§‘æ™®æ–‡æœ¬ï¼š

Scientists have discovered that bees communicate through a complex "dance language." When a worker bee finds food, it returns to the hive and performs specific movements. The round dance indicates food nearby, while the waggle dance provides information about distant sources. The direction and duration of the waggle show other bees exactly where to fly. These remarkable insects can even adjust their messages based on wind conditions and obstacles in the path.

Sarah hesitated before knocking on the old wooden door. The house had stood empty for years, its windows like vacant eyes staring across the neighborhood. Strange sounds had been reported by several neighbors, especially on windy nights like this one. Yet Sarah was determined to solve the mystery once and for all. She took a deep breath, raised her hand, and knocked three times. To her surprise, the door slowly opened by itself.
